SENTIENT SPECIES:
Feathered Koboldoids: Eat pretty much anything, including one another. Disturbingly fond of skulls. They have bilateral symmetry. They are hyperactive and have a deep need to conform. They first evolved on Hylus V in 1626.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: 1 CON: -1 INT: 1 CHA: 0
Six-Legged Red Robots: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have red skin. They have six legs. They have bilateral symmetry. They are humorless and always willing to listen. They were created by the Empire of Antoids and Robots on Aomep II as servants in 1641.
	Their Stats are: STR: 1 DEX: 1 CON: -1 INT: 0 CHA: 1
Six-Legged Black Antoids: Small, industrious and well-organised, these creatures' greatest weakness is their ever-ballooning population. They have black skin. They have six legs. They have bilateral symmetry. They are cautious and have a complex system of social castes. They were uplifted by the Fourth Church of Antoids and Humanoids on Krantor IV in 1225.
	Their Stats are: STR: 0 DEX: 1 CON: 2 INT: 0 CHA: -1
Feathered Robots: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have bilateral symmetry. They are modest and have a complex system of social rules. They were created by the Empire of Antoids and Robots on Wotan II as servants in 1642.
	Their Stats are: STR: -2 DEX: -1 CON: 2 INT: 1 CHA: -1

CIVILISATIONS:
THE REPUBLIC OF ROBOTS:
An ancient, corrupt, fantastically wealthy, highly advanced Republic of 4 planets, with 1 billion inhabitants.
Major populations:
1 billion Six-Legged Red Robots.
It is at peace with the Empire of Antoids and Robots.

	Their Stats are: STR: -4 DEX: -1 CON: -4 INT: -2 CHA: -2
THE EMPIRE OF ANTOIDS AND ROBOTS:
An ancient, corrupt, fantastically wealthy, highly advanced Empire of 23 planets, with 22 billion inhabitants.
Major populations:
19 billion Six-Legged Black Antoids.
2 billion enslaved Feathered Koboldoids.
1 billion enslaved Feathered Robots.
It controls a Universal Antidote.
It is at peace with the Republic of Robots.

	Their Stats are: STR: -3 DEX: 0 CON: -3 INT: -1 CHA: -1
PLANETS:

A barren planet of the Empire of Antoids and Robots.
It is a little polluted.
A mining base, built by the Empire of Antoids and Robots in 1679

GYNOW VI
A barren planet of the Republic of Robots.
It is heavily polluted.
A science lab, built by the Empire of Antoids and Robots in 1654
A block of time ice, encasing Unkut Igneous, Emperor of the Second Empire of Flying Trolloids created by the rogue AI Simulation 294 in 1337
Poison World: Mineral deposits produce a steady stream of toxins that makes survival extremely difficult.
Vast Empty Plains: Brown, dusty and featureless, their monotony is broken only by the occasional rivulet around which cluster many flying animals.
